CREATE_JOB_PROC
Create Or Replace Procedure Refres_Job_Proc Is 
								 Cursor C_Job Is Select Job From Sys.Dba_Jobs 
								                  Where Job <> 1 ;
								Begin
									For I In C_Job Loop
										Begin
										  Dbms_Job.Run(I.Job);
										Exception
								     When Others Then 
								       Null;
								    End ;
									End Loop ;		
								End ;
Alter  System Disable Restricted  Session
		Begin
		DBMS_SCHEDULER.CREATE_JOB(  JOB_NAME        => 'IAS_DATA_JOB',
																JOB_TYPE        => 'STORED_PROCEDURE',
																JOB_ACTION      => 'REFRES_JOB_PROC',
																START_DATE      =>  SYSTIMESTAMP,
																REPEAT_INTERVAL => 'SYSTIMESTAMP + INTERVAL ''1'' HOUR' ,
																END_DATE        => NULL ,
																COMMENTS        => 'Refresh Data',
																ENABLED         => TRUE);
		End ;

	  SR_NO       				 NUMBER(30)                       NOT NULL,
	  SR_SRL      				 NUMBER(38),
	  MSG_TYP  			     	 NUMBER(2)                        NOT NULL,
	  MSG_TXT    		    	 VARCHAR2(4000)            		    NOT NULL,
	  MOBILE_NO   			   VARCHAR2(20),
	  TO_EMAIL 						 VARCHAR2(100),
	  EMAIL_SUBJECT				 VARCHAR2(100),
	  DOC_TYP      			   NUMBER(10),
	  DOC_SRL        			 NUMBER(38),
	  PROCSSD_EMAIL_FLG    NUMBER(1)                        DEFAULT 0,
	  PROCSSD_SMS_FLG 		 NUMBER(1)                        DEFAULT 0,
	  SEND_DATE     			 DATE,
	  MSG_DATE       			 DATE                             DEFAULT SYSDATE,
	  AD_DATE        			 DATE                             DEFAULT SYSDATE,
	  CMP_NO     				   NUMBER(3),
	  BRN_NO        			 NUMBER(3),
	  BRN_USR       		   NUMBER(3),
	  BRN_YEAR      		   NUMBER(4) )

	  BRN_USR       NUMBER(3) ,

	  F_SYS           VARCHAR2 (15),
	  FORM_NO         NUMBER (5),

	  PRIMARY KEY ( FORM_NO )

	  TABLESPACE "IAS_SYS_DATA"

	  LANG_NO        NUMBER (2),
	  FORM_NO        NUMBER (5), 
	  FORM_NAME      VARCHAR2 (60),
	  CONSTRAINT S_SYSTEM_NAME_PK
	  PRIMARY KEY ( LANG_NO ,FORM_NO ) 
	  USING INDEX TABLESPACE "IAS_SYS_INDX",
	  CONSTRAINT S_SYSTEM_NAME_FK 
	  FOREIGN KEY (FORM_NO)  
	  REFERENCES  S_SYSTEM (FORM_NO) ON DELETE CASCADE)

CREATE TABLE S_FLAGS(
	  LANG_NO     NUMBER(2),
	  FLG_SR      NUMBER(5),

	  UP_DATE     DATE,
	  CONSTRAINT S_FLG_PK 
	  PRIMARY KEY (LANG_NO,FLG_CODE,FLG_VALUE))
	  TABLESPACE "IAS_SYS_DATA"

GET_CONS_NAME
SELECT A.CONSTRAINT_NAME   FROM USER_CONSTRAINTS A,USER_CONS_COLUMNS B  WHERE A.OWNER = B.OWNER  AND A.CONSTRAINT_NAME = B.CONSTRAINT_NAME  AND A.TABLE_NAME = B.TABLE_NAME  AND A.TABLE_NAME = DECODE(:b1, NULL ,A.TABLE_NAME,UPPER(:b1))  AND B.COLUMN_NAME = DECODE(:b3, NULL ,B.COLUMN_NAME,UPPER(:b3))  AND A.CONSTRAINT_TYPE = DECODE(:b5, NULL ,A.CONSTRAINT_TYPE,UPPER(:b5))  AND ROWNUM <= 1"

Main_Server.Info
Start CREATE  Mv itm_mov In User 
XXXXXXXXXX
Current User ==>>    
Start Create Synonym Item_Movement form User 
CREATE OR REPLACE  SYNONYM ITEM_MOVEMENT FOR 
.ITEM_MOVEMENT
Drop Snapshot MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY
Drop table MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY REFRESH  COMPLETE START WITH SYSDATE NEXT SYSDATE + 
 WITH PRIMARY KEY 
                  AS SELECT I_CODE, W_CODE, EXPIRE_DATE, BATCH_NO,SUM(ITM_QTY) AVL_QTY FROM (
                     SELECT  I_CODE, W_CODE, EXPIRE_DATE, BATCH_NO,SUM ((NVL (P_QTY, 0) + NVL (PF_QTY, 0)) * IN_OUT) ITM_QTY 
                    FROM ITEM_MOVEMENT
                      GROUP BY I_CODE,
                                W_CODE,
                                EXPIRE_DATE,
                                BATCH_NO  
                UNION ALL 
                     SELECT I_CODE,D.W_CODE,EXPIRE_DATE, BATCH_NO,  -(Sum(Nvl(P_qty,0))+Sum(Nvl(Free_Qty,0)*Nvl(P_Size,1)))  ITM_QTY
                      FROM IAS_POS_BILL_MST M,IAS_POS_BILL_DTL D
                                WHERE M.BILL_NO=D.BILL_NO				            
                                    AND NVL(POSTED,0)=0                             
                     GROUP BY I_CODE,
                              D.W_CODE,
                              EXPIRE_DATE,
                              BATCH_NO 
                UNION ALL 
                      SELECT I_CODE,D.W_CODE,EXPIRE_DATE, BATCH_NO,  (Sum(Nvl(P_qty,0))+Sum(Nvl(Free_Qty,0)*Nvl(P_Size,1)))  ITM_QTY
                        FROM IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST M,IAS_POS_RT_BILL_DTL D
				          WHERE M.RT_BILL_NO=D.RT_BILL_NO				            
				              AND NVL(POSTED,0)=0                             
                      GROUP BY I_CODE,
                               D.W_CODE,
                               EXPIRE_DATE,
                               BATCH_NO )
          GROUP BY I_CODE,
                  W_CODE,
                  EXPIRE_DATE,
                  BATCH_NO 
ALTER TABLE MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY ADD (CONSTRAINT PK_MV_ITEM_MOV PRIMARY KEY (i_code, w_code, expire_date, batch_no)) 
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW LOG ON MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY WITH ROWID INCLUDING NEW VALUES  
Insert into POS_SYNC_MNGMNT(TBL_NM, MV_NM, OWNR_TYP, RFRSH_TYP, UPDT_FLG, DLT_FLG, STP_RFRSH_FLG, MV_FLG, SYNNYM_FLG, SYS_NO,CTGRY_TYP)
		 Values('MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY', 'MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY', 1, 'ROWID', 0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 80, 5)
